The main distinguishing feature is ability to attach sound recording or photo to any data field regardless of its type. The data can be entered into individual records, or simultaneously into some of the fields of all selected records.\r\n\r\nThe application displays database records in customizable table and form views that share persistent settings for filtering and sorting. The display settings can be selected quickly by the name allowing easy changing of data view perspective.
